(**
   In this file, we show that an arbitrary weak equivalence F : C -> D preserves subobject classifiers.
 *)

Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Prelude.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Limits.Terminal.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Limits.Pullbacks.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Limits.Preservation.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Monics.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.WeakEquivalences.Core.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.WeakEquivalences.Terminal.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.WeakEquivalences.Mono.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.WeakEquivalences.Preservation.Pullbacks.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.WeakEquivalences.Reflection.Pullbacks.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.SubobjectClassifier.SubobjectClassifier.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.SubobjectClassifier.PreservesSubobjectClassifier.

Local Open Scope cat.

Section WeakEquivalencePreservationsSubobjectClassifier.

  Context {C D : category}
    {F : C ⟶ D}
    (Fw : is_weak_equiv F)
    {t_C : Terminal C}
    (t_D : Terminal D)
    (Ω : subobject_classifier t_C).

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
preserves_terminal F

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
preserves_terminal F

    
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
is_weak_equiv F

    exact Fw.
  Defined.

  Context {d₁ d₂ : D}
    {c₁ c₂ : C}
    (i₁ : z_iso (F c₁) d₁)
    (i₂ : z_iso (F c₂) d₂).

  Context (f : Monic D d₁ d₂).
  Let refl_f := reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f.
  Let const_tr₂ := TerminalArrow t_D d₁ · (TerminalArrow (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)).

  
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
t_F:= weak_equiv_preserves_terminal F Fw: preserves_terminal F
d₁, d₂: D
c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
φ: ∑ (χ : D ⟦ d₂, F Ω ⟧) (H : f · χ = const_tr₂),
isPullback H
i₁ · const_tr₂ = # F (const_true c₁ Ω)

· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧

isPullback H

  (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C) d₁ =
z_iso_inv i₁ · # F (TerminalArrow t_C c₁)
i₁
· (z_iso_inv i₁ · # F (TerminalArrow t_C c₁)
   · # F (pr12 Ω)) = ?b

c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
φ: ∑ (χ : D ⟦ d₂, F Ω ⟧) (H : f · χ = const_tr₂),
isPullback H
# F
  (fully_faithful_inv_hom (ff_from_weak_equiv F Fw) c₁
     Ω (i₁ · f · pr1 φ)) = # F (const_true c₁ Ω)

i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂

     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧

d': D
g: D ⟦ d', F c₂ ⟧
k: D ⟦ d', F t_C ⟧
pfₛ: g
· # F
    (invmap
       (weq_from_fully_faithful
          (ff_from_weak_equiv F Fw) c₂ Ω)
       (i₂ · pr1 ϕ)) = k · # F Ω
∃! hk : D ⟦ d', F c₁ ⟧,
hk · # F refl_f = g
× hk · # F (TerminalArrow t_C c₁) = k

d₁, d₂: D

i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
ϕ: ∑ (χ : D ⟦ d₂, F Ω ⟧) (H : f · χ = const_tr₂),
isPullback H
d': D
g: D ⟦ d', F c₂ ⟧
k: D ⟦ d', F t_C ⟧
pfₛ: g
· # F
    (invmap
       (weq_from_fully_faithful
          (ff_from_weak_equiv F Fw) c₂ Ω)
       (i₂ · pr1 ϕ)) = k · # F Ω
spf: g · i₂ · pr1 ϕ =
k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
R:= (pr22 ϕ) d' (g · i₂)
  (k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)) spf: ∃! hk : D ⟦ d', d₁ ⟧,
hk · f = g · i₂
× hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ =
  k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
∏ x : D ⟦ d', F c₁ ⟧,
(λ x0 : D ⟦ d', F c₁ ⟧,
 x0 · # F refl_f = g
 × x0 · # F (TerminalArrow t_C c₁) = k) x
≃ (λ y : D ⟦ d', d₁ ⟧,
   y · f = g · i₂
   × y · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ =
     k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)) 
    (?f x)

g: D ⟦ d', F c₂ ⟧
k: D ⟦ d', F t_C ⟧
pfₛ: g
· # F
    (invmap
       (weq_from_fully_faithful
          (ff_from_weak_equiv F Fw) c₂ Ω)
       (i₂ · pr1 ϕ)) = k · # F Ω
spf: g · i₂ · pr1 ϕ =
k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))

  (k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)) spf: ∃! hk : D ⟦ d', d₁ ⟧,
hk · f = g · i₂
× hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ =
  k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
x: D ⟦ d', F c₁ ⟧

· # F
    (fully_faithful_inv_hom 
       (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂
       (i₁ · f · inv_from_z_iso i₂)) = g
# F
  (fully_faithful_inv_hom (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂
     (i₁ · (f · inv_from_z_iso i₂))) =
i₁ · (f · z_iso_inv i₂)

       (weq_from_fully_faithful
          (ff_from_weak_equiv F Fw) c₂ Ω)
       (i₂ · pr1 ϕ)) = k · # F Ω
spf: g · i₂ · pr1 ϕ =
k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
R:= (pr22 ϕ) d' (g · i₂)
  (k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)) spf: ∃! hk : D ⟦ d', d₁ ⟧,
hk · f = g · i₂
× hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ =
  k · TerminalArrow t_D (F t_C)
x: D ⟦ d', F c₁ ⟧
isaprop
  (x
   · # F
       (fully_faithful_inv_hom (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂
          (i₁ · f · inv_from_z_iso i₂)) = g)
 apply homset_property.

isPullback H
pr1 φ₁ = pr1 φ₂

C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
t_F:= weak_equiv_preserves_terminal F Fw: preserves_terminal F
d₁, d₂: D
c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
d: D
g: D ⟦ d, d₂ ⟧
t: D ⟦ d, t_D ⟧
pf: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
t
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
tfc:= pr1 (t_F t_C (pr2 t_C) d): D ⟦ d, F t_C ⟧
pf₀: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
tfc · # F Ω
∃! hk : D ⟦ d, ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f ⟧,
hk · PullbackPr1 (ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f) =
g · z_iso_inv i₂
× hk · PullbackPr2 (ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f) =
  tfc

      exact (isPullback_Pullback (ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f) d (g · z_iso_inv i₂) tfc pf₀).

F: C ⟶ D

t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
t_F:= weak_equiv_preserves_terminal F Fw: preserves_terminal F
d₁, d₂: D
c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
d: D
g: D ⟦ d, d₂ ⟧
t: D ⟦ d, t_D ⟧
pf: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
t
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
tfc:= pr1 (t_F t_C (pr2 t_C) d): D ⟦ d, F t_C ⟧
pf₀: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
tfc · # F Ω
(∑ hk : D ⟦ d, ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f ⟧,
 hk · PullbackPr1 (ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f) =
 g · z_iso_inv i₂
 × hk
   · PullbackPr2 (ClassifyingPullbackOfImage refl_f) =
   tfc)
≃ (∑ hk : D ⟦ d, d₁ ⟧,
   hk · f = g × hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ = t)


    
C, D: category
F: C ⟶ D
Fw: is_weak_equiv F
t_C: Terminal C
t_D: Terminal D
Ω: subobject_classifier t_C
t_F:= weak_equiv_preserves_terminal F Fw: preserves_terminal F
d₁, d₂: D
c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
d: D
g: D ⟦ d, d₂ ⟧
t: D ⟦ d, t_D ⟧
pf: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
t
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
tfc:= pr1 (t_F t_C (pr2 t_C) d): D ⟦ d, F t_C ⟧
pf₀: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
tfc · # F Ω
(∑
 hk : D ⟦ d,
      make_Pullback
        (functor_on_square C D F
           (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                    refl_f)))
        (weak_equiv_preserves_pullbacks Fw c₂ t_C Ω
           (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f)
           (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) Ω
           (PullbackPr1
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (PullbackPr2
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (PullbackSqrCommutes
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (functor_on_square C D F
              (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                       refl_f)))
           (isPullback_Pullback
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f)))
      ⟧,
 hk
 · PullbackPr1
     (make_Pullback
        (functor_on_square C D F
           (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                    refl_f)))
        (weak_equiv_preserves_pullbacks Fw c₂ t_C Ω
           (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f)
           (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) Ω
           (PullbackPr1
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (PullbackPr2
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (PullbackSqrCommutes
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f))
           (functor_on_square C D F
              (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                       refl_f)))
           (isPullback_Pullback
              (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f)))) =
 g · z_iso_inv i₂
 × hk
   · PullbackPr2
       (make_Pullback
          (functor_on_square C D F
             (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                      refl_f)))
          (weak_equiv_preserves_pullbacks Fw c₂ t_C Ω
             (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω refl_f)
             (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) Ω
             (PullbackPr1
                (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                   refl_f))
             (PullbackPr2
                (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                   refl_f))
             (PullbackSqrCommutes
                (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                   refl_f))
             (functor_on_square C D F
                (pr12 (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                         refl_f)))
             (isPullback_Pullback
                (subobject_classifier_pullback Ω
                   refl_f)))) = tfc)
≃ (∑ hk : D ⟦ d, d₁ ⟧,
   hk · f = g × hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ = t)

t_C: Terminal C

t_F:= weak_equiv_preserves_terminal F Fw: preserves_terminal F
d₁, d₂: D
c₁, c₂: C
i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
d: D
g: D ⟦ d, d₂ ⟧
t: D ⟦ d, t_D ⟧
pf: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
t
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
tfc:= pr1 (t_F t_C (pr2 t_C) d): D ⟦ d, F t_C ⟧
pf₀: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
tfc · # F Ω
(∑ hk : D ⟦ d, F c₁ ⟧,
 hk
 · # F
     (invmap (weq_from_fully_faithful (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂)
        (i₁ · f · inv_from_z_iso i₂)) =
 g · inv_from_z_iso i₂
 × hk · # F (TerminalArrow t_C c₁) = tfc)
≃ (∑ hk : D ⟦ d, d₁ ⟧,
   hk · f = g × hk · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ = t)

   y · f = g × y · TerminalArrow t_D d₁ = t) 
    (?f x)

    (invmap (weq_from_fully_faithful (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂)
       (i₁ · f · inv_from_z_iso i₂)) =
g · inv_from_z_iso i₂ ≃ x · i₁ · f = g

i₁: z_iso (F c₁) d₁
i₂: z_iso (F c₂) d₂
f: Monic D d₁ d₂
refl_f:= reflection_of_mono (pr2 Fw) i₁ i₂ f: Monic C c₁ c₂
const_tr₂:= TerminalArrow t_D d₁
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F
        t_C) t_D · # F (pr12 Ω)): D ⟦ d₁, F (pr1 Ω) ⟧
d: D
g: D ⟦ d, d₂ ⟧
t: D ⟦ d, t_D ⟧
pf: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
t
· (TerminalArrow
     (preserves_terminal_to_terminal F t_F t_C)
     t_D · # F (pr12 Ω))
tfc:= pr1 (t_F t_C (pr2 t_C) d): D ⟦ d, F t_C ⟧
pf₀: g · z_iso_inv i₂
· # F (characteristic_morphism Ω refl_f) =
tfc · # F Ω
x: D ⟦ d, F c₁ ⟧
pq: x · i₁ · f = g
x
· # F
    (invmap (weq_from_fully_faithful (pr2 Fw) c₁ c₂)
       (i₁ · f · inv_from_z_iso i₂)) = ?b
